RedirectMatch 301 /registration/(.*) /account/$1
RedirectMatch 301 /registration(.*) /account/$1
RedirectMatch 301 /store/(.*) /Shop-Pit-Boss/Accessories/$1
RedirectMatch 301 /pellets/(.*) /Shop-Pit-Boss/Fuel/$1
# 301 --- /products/?product=* => /shop-pit-boss/grills/*
RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} (^|&)product\=\*($|&)
RewriteRule ^products/$ /shop\-pit\-boss/grills/*? [L,R=301]
